Brookfield Renewable operates one of the world’s largest publicly traded, pure-play renewable power platforms. Our portfolio consists of hydroelectric, wind, solar and storage facilities in North America, South America, Europe and Asia, and totals approximately 23,000 megawatts of installed capacity and an approximately 75,000-megawatt and 8 million metric tons per annum of carbon dioxide (“MMTPA CO2”) development pipeline. (NYSE: BEP; TSX: BEP.UN), a Bermuda-based limited partnership, or Brookfield Renewable Corporation (NYSE, TSX: BEPC), a Canadian corporation. Join our team to contribute to the success of one of the fastest growing and largest publicly traded, pure play renewable power platforms in the world while supporting decarbonization and greater energy sustainability to facilitate the global transition to a net-zero economy.<\u002Fp> \n    <p><b> Summary<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n    <p> Reporting to the Senior Procurement Manager, the Procurement networking, and telecom agreements)<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Develop sourcing strategies that maximize value and mitigate risks to the company and its clients<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Work with IT functional \n    <p> Brookfield Renewable operates one of the world’s largest publicly traded, pure-play renewable power platforms. Our portfolio consists of hydroelectric, wind, solar and storage facilities in North America, South America, Europe and Asia, and totals approximately 23,000 megawatts of installed capacity and an approximately 75,000-megawatt and 8 million metric tons per annum of carbon dioxide (“MMTPA CO2”) development pipeline. Investors can access its portfolio either through Brookfield Renewable Partners L.P. (NYSE: BEP; TSX: BEP.UN), a Bermuda-based limited partnership, or Brookfield Renewable Corporation (NYSE, TSX: BEPC), a Canadian corporation. Further information is available at https:\u002F\u002Fbep.brookfield.com. Important information may be disseminated exclusively via the website; investors should consult the site to access this information. Brookfield Renewable is the flagship listed renewable power company of Brookfield Asset Management.<\u002Fp> \n    <p> At Brookfield Renewable, we attract and retain high-performing individuals who are interested in making an impact and being part of a fast-paced and collaborative environment. Join our team to contribute to the success of one of the fastest growing and largest publicly traded, pure play renewable power platforms in the world while supporting decarbonization and greater energy sustainability to facilitate the global transition to a net-zero economy.<\u002Fp> \n    <p><b> Position Summary<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n    <p> Reporting to the Director, Procurement, the Procurement Manager is responsible for procurement activities related to the sourcing, negotiation and implementation of Engineering, Procurement and Construction agreements for the development of utility-scale renewable energy sites across North America as well as the sourcing of major equipment and the and negotiation of Long-Term Services Agreements required for the operation and maintenance of these sites.<\u002Fp> \n    <p><b> Responsibilities<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n    <ul> \n     <li>Work closely with the Business Development team on utility-scale solar development and repower projects across North America<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Liaise with the Technical team to obtain and verify technical specifications<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Prepare all commercial bid documents including contractual terms and conditions with support from Legal Counsel<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Develop bid evaluation matrix with support from the technical team<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Manage the entire bid process by:<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Leading RFP kickoff meeting with all relevant stakeholders<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Managing and maintaining the integrity of the bid process<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Coordinating technical evaluations and conducting commercial evaluations including normalization of all compliant proposals<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Preparing a final vendor recommendation for senior management<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Reviewing all comments and exceptions taken to the proposed form of agreement and working with Legal Counsel to negotiate a final agreement<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Develop strong relationships with a network of EPC Contractors across North America<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Stay current with market requirements, resources, pricing and trends.<\u002Fli> \n    <\u002Ful> \n    <p><b>Requirements<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n    <ul> \n     <li>7-10 years Procurement experience, with 5+ years of experience in Renewable Energy with a focus on utility-scale development collaboration and values in-office interactions. We believe that it is beneficial for employees to be in the office to ensure that we provide the appropriate training and coaching, facilitate real-time learning through direct interactions with colleagues and senior leaders via our open concept environment, and accelerate the integration of new employees into our teams. As we transition back to the office, we are currently offering a hybrid work environment with a minimum of 3 days in office, and we will reassess the approach on a as needed basis.<\u002Fp> \n    <p> <i>Brookfield Renewable embraces and promotes the principles of diversity, equity and inclusion. Brookfield Renewable operates one of the world’s largest publicly traded, pure-play renewable power platforms. Our portfolio consists of hydroelectric, wind, solar and storage facilities in North America, South America, Europe and Asia, and totals approximately 23,000 megawatts of installed capacity and an approximately 75,000-megawatt and 8 million metric tons per annum of carbon dioxide (“MMTPA CO2”) development pipeline. Investors can access its portfolio either through Brookfield Renewable Partners L.P. (NYSE: BEP; TSX: BEP.UN), a Bermuda-based limited partnership, or Brookfield Renewable Corporation (NYSE, TSX: BEPC), a Canadian corporation. Further information is available at https:\u002F\u002Fbep.brookfield.com. Important information may be disseminated exclusively via the website; investors should consult the site to access this information. Brookfield Renewable is the flagship listed renewable power company of Brookfield Asset Management.<\u002Fp> \n    <p><b> Summary<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n    <p> Reporting to the Senior Director, Corporate Operations within the Technical Services Group, the Solar Engineer is responsible for providing technical support to the business and advise on solar opportunities globally. Technical expertise of the candidate will be such to support at very different project stages ranging from early development, construction, commissioning and operation. The Solar engineer will provide technical assessment on M&amp;A and acquisition of solar projects to support the growth strategy of the business.<\u002Fp> \n    <p><b> Responsibilities<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n    <ul> \n     <li>Conduct the screening, feasibility studies, prioritization and due diligence of potential solar projects;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Undertake solar PV resource and energy yield analyses including review of irradiation data, PV system design and uncertainty analysis;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Work with the Investment team to assess global opportunities to acquire solar facilities and project pipelines for development;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Develop and implement global procedures, guidelines and best practices for solar development and operations in collaboration with local engineering teams;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Support the development of technical specifications and quality assessment for procurement and operation of main solar components;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Lead global technical working groups that analyze field experience and research developments in the solar industry and report findings\u002Fsolutions;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Understanding and assessment of plant performance indicators to identify and lead global performance improvement initiatives;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Share best practices that apply to the design, construction, operation and asset management of facilities;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Conduct comparative technical and commercial analyses of equipment suppliers and establish corporate relationships at global level.<\u002Fli>\n    <\u002Ful>\n    <br> \n    <p><\u002Fp> \n    <p><b> Requirements<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n    <ul> \n     <li>Solid knowledge of leading key equipment suppliers for solar projects, with understanding of bankability, warranties and quality assessment procedures;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Good understanding of key items of EPC and O&amp;M contracts;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Deep understanding of engineering design and cost optimization of solar projects ready to build;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Knowledge of global technical standards and requirements applicable to design, safety and construction of solar plants. Appreciation of the economics of solar energy development;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Experience in conducting due diligence of development and operational solar projects to support project financing initiatives;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Proven ability to develop strong business relationships with internal and external stakeholders;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Excellent written and verbal communication skills in Spanish and English;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Ability to work with multinational teams with varying time zones in a dynamic, fast-paced environment and to adapt quickly to changing priorities;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Position will be based in our Madrid office. Some international travel required.<\u002Fli> \n    <\u002Ful> \n    <p><b>Qualifications<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n    <ul> \n     <li>Bachelor’s Degree in Engineering, Physics, or Material Science;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Technical competency and experience (minimum 5 years) with the design and construction of utility scale solar projects;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Knowledge of solar energy production processes gained through Operations, Development, or Engineering support;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Experience in PV simulation tools (PVSyst, SAM);<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Experience with grid connection and power electronics would be an asset;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Desired knowledge and\u002For working experience with Data Management, Analytical and Statistical tools;<\u002Fli> \n     <li>Excellent organizational skills, including the ability to identify priorities and plan work independently while managing competing deadlines.<\u002Fli> \n    <\u002Ful> \n    <p>At Brookfield Renewable, we attract and retain high-performing individuals who are interested in making an impact and being part of a fast-paced and collaborative environment. Join our team to contribute to the success of one of the fastest growing and largest publicly traded, pure play renewable power platforms in the world while supporting decarbonization and greater energy sustainability to facilitate the global transition to a net-zero economy.<\u002Fp> \n    <p> Brookfield has a strong culture that focuses on collaboration and values in-office interactions. We believe that it is beneficial for employees to be in the office to ensure that we provide the appropriate training and coaching, facilitate real-time learning through direct interactions with colleagues and senior leaders via our open concept environment, and accelerate the integration of new employees into our teams. (NYSE: BEP; TSX: BEP.UN), a Bermuda-based limited partnership, or Brookfield Renewable Corporation (NYSE, TSX: BEPC), a Canadian corporation. Further information is available at https:\u002F\u002Fbep.brookfield.com. Important information may be disseminated exclusively via the website; investors should consult the site to access this information.
